alternative(PCI_GOANY_alt, PCI_GOBIOS, PCI_GOMMCONFIG, PCI_GODIRECT, PCI_GOOLPC, PCI_GOANY)
	13
	BV_5 = [0,1]=>SUM ([PCI_GOANY + PCI_GOOLPC + PCI_GODIRECT + PCI_GOMMCONFIG + PCI_GOBIOS = 1]), !BV_5 = [0,1]=>SUM ([PCI_GOANY + PCI_GOOLPC + PCI_GODIRECT + PCI_GOMMCONFIG + PCI_GOBIOS != 1])
	BV_6 = [0,1]=>SUM ([PCI_GOANY + PCI_GOOLPC + PCI_GODIRECT + PCI_GOMMCONFIG + PCI_GOBIOS != 1]), !BV_6 = [0,1]=>SUM ([PCI_GOANY + PCI_GOOLPC + PCI_GODIRECT + PCI_GOMMCONFIG + PCI_GOBIOS = 1])
	ARITHM ([PCI_GOANY_alt + not(PCI_GOBIOS) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([PCI_GOANY_alt + not(PCI_GOMMCONFIG) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([PCI_GOANY_alt + not(PCI_GODIRECT) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([PCI_GOANY_alt + not(PCI_GOOLPC) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([PCI_GOANY_alt + not(PCI_GOANY) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([not(PCI_GOANY_alt) + BV_5 >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_5 + not(PCI_GOBIOS) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_5 + not(PCI_GOMMCONFIG) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_5 + not(PCI_GODIRECT) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_5 + not(PCI_GOOLPC) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_5 + not(PCI_GOANY) >= 1])

alternative(VMSPLIT_3G_OPT_alt, VMSPLIT_3G, VMSPLIT_3G_OPT, VMSPLIT_2G, VMSPLIT_2G_OPT, VMSPLIT_1G)
	13
	BV_7 = [0,1]=>SUM ([VMSPLIT_1G + VMSPLIT_2G_OPT + VMSPLIT_2G + VMSPLIT_3G_OPT + VMSPLIT_3G = 1]), !BV_7 = [0,1]=>SUM ([VMSPLIT_1G + VMSPLIT_2G_OPT + VMSPLIT_2G + VMSPLIT_3G_OPT + VMSPLIT_3G != 1])
	BV_8 = [0,1]=>SUM ([VMSPLIT_1G + VMSPLIT_2G_OPT + VMSPLIT_2G + VMSPLIT_3G_OPT + VMSPLIT_3G != 1]), !BV_8 = [0,1]=>SUM ([VMSPLIT_1G + VMSPLIT_2G_OPT + VMSPLIT_2G + VMSPLIT_3G_OPT + VMSPLIT_3G = 1])
	ARITHM ([VMSPLIT_3G_OPT_alt + not(VMSPLIT_3G) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([VMSPLIT_3G_OPT_alt + not(VMSPLIT_3G_OPT) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([VMSPLIT_3G_OPT_alt + not(VMSPLIT_2G) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([VMSPLIT_3G_OPT_alt + not(VMSPLIT_2G_OPT) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([VMSPLIT_3G_OPT_alt + not(VMSPLIT_1G) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([not(VMSPLIT_3G_OPT_alt) + BV_7 >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_7 + not(VMSPLIT_3G) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_7 + not(VMSPLIT_3G_OPT) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_7 + not(VMSPLIT_2G) >= 1])

alternative(DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK_alt, DEFAULT_SECURITY_SELINUX, DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK, DEFAULT_SECURITY_TOMOYO, DEFAULT_SECURITY_DAC)
	11
	BV_13 = [0,1]=>SUM ([DEFAULT_SECURITY_DAC + DEFAULT_SECURITY_TOMOYO + DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK + DEFAULT_SECURITY_SELINUX = 1]), !BV_13 = [0,1]=>SUM ([DEFAULT_SECURITY_DAC + DEFAULT_SECURITY_TOMOYO + DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK + DEFAULT_SECURITY_SELINUX != 1])
	BV_14 = [0,1]=>SUM ([DEFAULT_SECURITY_DAC + DEFAULT_SECURITY_TOMOYO + DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK + DEFAULT_SECURITY_SELINUX != 1]), !BV_14 = [0,1]=>SUM ([DEFAULT_SECURITY_DAC + DEFAULT_SECURITY_TOMOYO + DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK + DEFAULT_SECURITY_SELINUX = 1])
	ARITHM ([DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK_alt + not(DEFAULT_SECURITY_SELINUX) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK_alt + not(DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK_alt + not(DEFAULT_SECURITY_TOMOYO) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK_alt + not(DEFAULT_SECURITY_DAC) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([not(DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK_alt) + BV_13 >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_13 + not(DEFAULT_SECURITY_SELINUX) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_13 + not(DEFAULT_SECURITY_SMACK) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_13 + not(DEFAULT_SECURITY_TOMOYO) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_13 + not(DEFAULT_SECURITY_DAC) >= 1])

alternative(USB_MUSB_HOST_alt, USB_MUSB_HOST, USB_MUSB_PERIPHERAL, USB_MUSB_OTG)
	9
	BV_43 = [0,1]=>SUM ([USB_MUSB_OTG + USB_MUSB_PERIPHERAL + USB_MUSB_HOST = 1]), !BV_43 = [0,1]=>SUM ([USB_MUSB_OTG + USB_MUSB_PERIPHERAL + USB_MUSB_HOST != 1])
	BV_44 = [0,1]=>SUM ([USB_MUSB_OTG + USB_MUSB_PERIPHERAL + USB_MUSB_HOST != 1]), !BV_44 = [0,1]=>SUM ([USB_MUSB_OTG + USB_MUSB_PERIPHERAL + USB_MUSB_HOST = 1])
	ARITHM ([USB_MUSB_HOST_alt + not(USB_MUSB_HOST) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([USB_MUSB_HOST_alt + not(USB_MUSB_PERIPHERAL) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([USB_MUSB_HOST_alt + not(USB_MUSB_OTG) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([not(USB_MUSB_HOST_alt) + BV_43 >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_43 + not(USB_MUSB_HOST) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_43 + not(USB_MUSB_PERIPHERAL) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_43 + not(USB_MUSB_OTG) >= 1])

	BV_70 = [0,1]=>SUM ([MMC_S3C_PIODMA + MMC_S3C_DMA + MMC_S3C_PIO != 1]), !BV_70 = [0,1]=>SUM ([MMC_S3C_PIODMA + MMC_S3C_DMA + MMC_S3C_PIO = 1])
	ARITHM ([MMC_S3C_PIO_alt + not(MMC_S3C_PIO) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([MMC_S3C_PIO_alt + not(MMC_S3C_DMA) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([MMC_S3C_PIO_alt + not(MMC_S3C_PIODMA) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([not(MMC_S3C_PIO_alt) + BV_69 >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_69 + not(MMC_S3C_PIO) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_69 + not(MMC_S3C_DMA) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_69 + not(MMC_S3C_PIODMA) >= 1])

alternative(B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE_alt, B43LEGACY_DMA_AND_PIO_MODE, B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE, B43LEGACY_PIO_MODE)
	9
	BV_73 = [0,1]=>SUM ([B43LEGACY_PIO_MODE + B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE + B43LEGACY_DMA_AND_PIO_MODE = 1]), !BV_73 = [0,1]=>SUM ([B43LEGACY_PIO_MODE + B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE + B43LEGACY_DMA_AND_PIO_MODE != 1])
	BV_74 = [0,1]=>SUM ([B43LEGACY_PIO_MODE + B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE + B43LEGACY_DMA_AND_PIO_MODE != 1]), !BV_74 = [0,1]=>SUM ([B43LEGACY_PIO_MODE + B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE + B43LEGACY_DMA_AND_PIO_MODE = 1])
	ARITHM ([B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE_alt + not(B43LEGACY_DMA_AND_PIO_MODE) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE_alt + not(B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE_alt + not(B43LEGACY_PIO_MODE) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([not(B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE_alt) + BV_73 >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_73 + not(B43LEGACY_DMA_AND_PIO_MODE) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_73 + not(B43LEGACY_DMA_MODE) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_73 + not(B43LEGACY_PIO_MODE) >= 1])

	7
	BV_75 = [0,1]=>ARITHM ([STMMAC_TMU_TIMER = [0,1] + STMMAC_RTC_TIMER = [0,1] = 1]), !BV_75 = [0,1]=>ARITHM ([PropNotEqualXY_C(STMMAC_TMU_TIMER, STMMAC_RTC_TIMER)])
	BV_76 = [0,1]=>ARITHM ([PropNotEqualXY_C(STMMAC_TMU_TIMER, STMMAC_RTC_TIMER)]), !BV_76 = [0,1]=>ARITHM ([STMMAC_TMU_TIMER = [0,1] + STMMAC_RTC_TIMER = [0,1] = 1])
	ARITHM ([STMMAC_TMU_TIMER_alt + not(STMMAC_TMU_TIMER) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([STMMAC_TMU_TIMER_alt + not(STMMAC_RTC_TIMER) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([not(STMMAC_TMU_TIMER_alt) + BV_75 >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_75 + not(STMMAC_TMU_TIMER) >= 1])

alternative(DEFAULT_NOOP_alt, DEFAULT_DEADLINE, DEFAULT_CFQ, DEFAULT_NOOP)
	9
	BV_77 = [0,1]=>SUM ([DEFAULT_NOOP + DEFAULT_CFQ + DEFAULT_DEADLINE = 1]), !BV_77 = [0,1]=>SUM ([DEFAULT_NOOP + DEFAULT_CFQ + DEFAULT_DEADLINE != 1])
	BV_78 = [0,1]=>SUM ([DEFAULT_NOOP + DEFAULT_CFQ + DEFAULT_DEADLINE != 1]), !BV_78 = [0,1]=>SUM ([DEFAULT_NOOP + DEFAULT_CFQ + DEFAULT_DEADLINE = 1])
	ARITHM ([DEFAULT_NOOP_alt + not(DEFAULT_DEADLINE) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([DEFAULT_NOOP_alt + not(DEFAULT_CFQ) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([DEFAULT_NOOP_alt + not(DEFAULT_NOOP) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([not(DEFAULT_NOOP_alt) + BV_77 >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_77 + not(DEFAULT_DEADLINE) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_77 + not(DEFAULT_CFQ) >= 1])
	ARITHM ([BV_77 + not(DEFAULT_NOOP) >= 1])
